<div id="review_467077255" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/467077255" />
    <a title="Mia Asher" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12676946-mia-asher"><img alt="Mia Asher" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442890061p2/12676946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/467077255?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mia Asher" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mia Asher" href="/user/show/12676946-mia-asher">Mia Asher</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467077255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7207267588538470427">"I feel like I've died and gone to hottie heaven." - Keatyn<br/><br/>This is how Keatyn feels when she arrives to her boarding school, a place that will be her home for the next year of her life, and it is NOT a joke. It is a Hottie Heaven that only Jillian Dodd could create so well. When I finished reading Stalk me (vol. 1), I was left with an amazing feeling that I had just walked into my teenage dream of going to a boarding school with hot boys and, well, have fun. Keatyn arrives to this boarding schoo</span>
  <span id="freeText7207267588538470427" style="display:none">"I feel like I've died and gone to hottie heaven." - Keatyn<br /><br />This is how Keatyn feels when she arrives to her boarding school, a place that will be her home for the next year of her life, and it is NOT a joke. It is a Hottie Heaven that only Jillian Dodd could create so well. When I finished reading Stalk me (vol. 1), I was left with an amazing feeling that I had just walked into my teenage dream of going to a boarding school with hot boys and, well, have fun. Keatyn arrives to this boarding school and is suddenly introduced to so many boys at once, and well, you CANNOT help but wonder who will be the boy to steal her heart. Trust the possibilities are endless and you will definitely be rooting for one team in particular, or as in my case, TEAMS.<br /><br />&lt;3 Team Dallas and Team Aiden &lt;3<br /><br />Do NOT be fooled though... This is not a book about a girl meets boy and falls in love AT ALL, it is so much more. This is a coming-of-age story where a girl, who was not sure if she liked herself that well to begin with (Stalk Me), is sent to boarding school due to certain circumstances that happen in Stalk me...it has to do with the title of the book. Anyway, in Kiss me, the reader will begin to see the transformation of Keatyn into someone that will be proud of her own achievements, decisions in life, and, maybe, fall in love. You begin to see her become a girl that is so likable that when you are inside her head (the book is written in first person so you are always inside her head) you cannot stop yourself from grinning. So much so that your cheeks will hurt. Keatyn doesn't lose one bit of her fantastic/bigger than life personality from Stalk me, but what the reader discovers in Kiss me is that she has sooo more many layers to her pesonality that make her soo unique and so Keatyn. What I mean is that You don't get to fully appreciate her in Stalk me. In Kiss me, you get to see that she is sweet/sexy/playful/spunky/funny/charismatic/confused/damaged... she is a REAL teenager.<br /><br />I won't give details about the plot because you NEED TO READ this book but what I will tell you is that if you enjoy real teenage voices, with extremely well developed characters, and an amazing and well-thought-out plot this is THE book for you.<br /><br />Jillian Dodd's writing is relevant, witty, playful, hilarious, and very current. You'll get your analogies and your deep writing but in a fun and very, very witty way. You will laugh your butt off when you read this book, you will sigh and want to swoon... you will fan yourself with the closest thing to you because the boys are so hot... you will cry with Keatyn.. and you will be AFRAID for her too... This is a phenomenal book. And you do not want to miss it.<br /><br />One last thing, Teenagers and parents should read this book together!!!! It deals with very relevant issues that teenagers face such as being able to communicate openly with their parents, sex, and popularity. It is a beautiful book with sooo many beautiful messages underneath all the fun, wittiness, and lightness that characterizes the author's writing.<br /><br />Bravo, Jillian Dodd.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7207267588538470427" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_466308761" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/466308761" />
    <a title="Britt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2196186-britt"><img alt="Britt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1349958146p2/2196186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/466308761?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Britt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Britt" href="/user/show/2196186-britt">Britt</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer466308761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11066530761137494037"><b> 4 stars </b><br/><br/>I loved this book so much more than the first, however once again I felt like I shouldn’t have. <br/><br/>So I have said it a million times but I will say it again. I HATE LOVE TRIANGLES. The reason for this is someone always has to miss out, or neither of them in the end, or if the author is a masochist she just kills one of the characters off. The only thing that gets me past a love triangle normally is those books such as the first in this series Stalk Me and Between the Lines by Tammara Webbe</span>
  <span id="freeText11066530761137494037" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars </b><br /><br />I loved this book so much more than the first, however once again I felt like I shouldn’t have. <br /><br />So I have said it a million times but I will say it again. I HATE LOVE TRIANGLES. The reason for this is someone always has to miss out, or neither of them in the end, or if the author is a masochist she just kills one of the characters off. The only thing that gets me past a love triangle normally is those books such as the first in this series Stalk Me and Between the Lines by Tammara Webber where I can’t stand one character. So as long as they end up with who I want them to end up with me I am happy as Larry. <br /><br /> The reason I didn’t like this book: I COULD NOT CHOOSE. Usually when I do face the love triangle scenario, for example in The Hunger Games and Twilight I end up falling down on one side. This is probably the first time where I am TEAM AIDEN <b> and </b> TEAM DAWSON. Although I must say I am definitely not Team Dallas or Team Damian because I really don’t see a romantic relationship with these two. They are friends (even though she does kiss Dallas), they should stay friends in my honest opinion. <br /><br />In a way I know where Dodd is going with this. I know that eventually Team Aiden is going to win. It’s inevitable so I’m mentally preparing myself to cry for Dawson but also be happy for Aiden. I am kind of wishing that Dawson has an asshole moment or turns out to be gay or cheats on her or something that I don’t have to feel sorry for him. Do you see now what this book is doing to my head? Although that said even if Team Aiden does win out, the way that this series has been going there will be a new team to join after Aiden turns out to be a dick. I sure hope not. <br /><br />As you can probably tell from my rather ranty thoughts this book is drama filled. It centres around drama. The thing I loved the most about this book is that I think Keatyn grows as a person. I had a love/hate relationship with her in the first book, but in this book it’s more on the love side of things as she does become less annoying and I like how she shuns popularity rather than strives for it.<br /><br />Having experienced high school myself with a lot of guy friends I really enjoyed the platonic relationship between her, Riley and Dallas. It was nice and made me smile. I want to be their best friends too!<br /><br />This is one of those books I love to hate. But boy can I not wait to read more!!!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11066530761137494037" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer431743699" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14862205570917515459">So loved this book. I think I even loved it more than the first. Is that even possible because Stalk me was EPIC! So what does that make Kiss Me?-- UBER EPIC? It probably doesn't even matter. Except that you so need to read this book!!! Jillian Dodd is like the Goddess of mature YA lit-- she just gets it. <br/>Kiss Me, the second book to the Keatyn Chronicles, was so much fun. There is still the God of All Hotties making his play on Keatyn but then there's Dawson. OMG-- I personally think he should h</span>
  <span id="freeText14862205570917515459" style="display:none">So loved this book. I think I even loved it more than the first. Is that even possible because Stalk me was EPIC! So what does that make Kiss Me?-- UBER EPIC? It probably doesn't even matter. Except that you so need to read this book!!! Jillian Dodd is like the Goddess of mature YA lit-- she just gets it. <br />Kiss Me, the second book to the Keatyn Chronicles, was so much fun. There is still the God of All Hotties making his play on Keatyn but then there's Dawson. OMG-- I personally think he should have the title of God of All Hotties. But whatever -- he's just HOT!!! And he and Keatyn totally click. But what's a girl to do -- it's so confusing with all the hotness right at your finger tips. I'm not sure I would be able to keep a clear head to try and figure out how my life has changed and what hottie i should be with and oh-- that stalker guy, Vincent is still a presence - um scary. Life at boarding school seems cool. I mean there's of course the bitch Whitney but whatever. She's gonna do what she does.<br />So back to J Dodd --- being the goddess that she is, wrote a fun, sexy, HOT, well really HOT actually, not too angsty, damn fab book!!! All her characters are so much fun. And-- they totally remind you of what it was like to be that young again. The fashion is to die for -- so want to raid Keatyn's closet. And where were the Gods of All Hotties when I was in high school? The story isn't too heavy-- well except for that whole Vincent stalker bit -- but Keatyn is being well protected. You fall in love with this story cuz it's light. You laugh, you SQUEEE and OMG -- the sweet things those boys do for Keatyn-- even Riley and Dallas who are HOT but they're just Keats' friends who are great kissers. And Keatyn- um who would't want to be her friend. She is so witty, and she is so not whiny. She's strong but she's a girl and has feelings. I love her. She's one of the best young female characters in any books.<br />If you're looking for a fun night and something laid back-- totally read Kiss Me. It's so good and did I mention HOT? Cuz ya-- HOT!!! -- that is all.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/498614528?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.C. MacKenzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.C. MacKenzie" href="/user/show/7555250-c-c-mackenzie">C.C. MacKenzie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer498614528" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17837766339360919413">Did you guys ever watch Gossip Girl? Or Beverly Hills 90210 in the early days?<br/><br/>Well, if you enjoyed those, you’re going to love the steamy Keatyn Chronicles. Readers have gone wild for Keatyn and her complicated life, never mind her even more complex love life.<br/><br/>Jillian’s ability to write such a fabulously drawn character has readers coming back for more again and again. Keatyn may look as if she has it all, but she hasn’t and she has the smarts to know it too. This is no timid little doormat. This</span>
  <span id="freeText17837766339360919413" style="display:none">Did you guys ever watch Gossip Girl? Or Beverly Hills 90210 in the early days?<br /><br />Well, if you enjoyed those, you’re going to love the steamy Keatyn Chronicles. Readers have gone wild for Keatyn and her complicated life, never mind her even more complex love life.<br /><br />Jillian’s ability to write such a fabulously drawn character has readers coming back for more again and again. Keatyn may look as if she has it all, but she hasn’t and she has the smarts to know it too. This is no timid little doormat. This is a girl who’s on life’s journey to understand herself, her sexuality, to figure out where she fits in to a perplexing world and how she deals with being separated from all she holds dear.<br /><br />It’s the sign of a great author when he/she deals effortlessly with a protagonist’s flaws. And Keatyn has plenty, which made me laugh out loud at times and brought a lump to my throat, too.<br /><br />The secondary characters are incredibly well written, especially the guys. The men are so drool worthy, fans of Keatyn are busy on social networking sites posting photos of who they think should play them in a film or television series. And right there is the magic. I wouldn’t be surprised to see a television series in the books’ future.<br /><br />There’s plenty more to come from Jillian and I cannot wait.<br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3648326518774193066">The Keatyn Chronicles - Book 2<br/><br/>Can I just say that I absolutely love Jillian Dodd and the her Keatyn Chronicles series!   <span id="freeText3648326518774193066" style="display:none">The Keatyn Chronicles - Book 2<br /><br />Can I just say that I absolutely love Jillian Dodd and the her Keatyn Chronicles series! I hate when the books end because I want more!! <br /><br />In Kiss Me, we pick up right where Stalk Me left off. Keatyn is at boarding school with a new life, new friends and new boys! Quite a few of them! I think at one point I was actually confused with ALL of the boys, Riley, Dallas, Dawson, Aiden and let's not forget about Brooklyn (though he's on my shit list right now). While I'm still Team Aiden (demi-God of all hotties), Dawson was sweet, sexy and charming just not who I see Keatyn with for the rest of the series. They do have a cute relationship but I'm just waiting for Aiden to step it up a notch! Aiden does have his swoon-worthy moments, especially his song list! He is the perfect blend of sweetness and bad boy! <br /><br />Can't wait to read more in Date Me!<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://teahoneysbookcafe.blogspot.com/">http://teahoneysbookcafe.blogspot.com/</a></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EtgdwQQgo5inR0vk17WRTAcay55tusPRJMVhcTjcqkOLpcPPFPVGnSdXkO/l4FlkhauIhKKSinBl+lnhD/M0oA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wNJ2Jp/ApMg1EVKxEELlhYLBYbIvxDUvUBNa9NwjybFZr6gojxVBzbUBiboiFy2tAHAiqODsfI4RLGJk6wxXUg==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText4127200400755998599" style="display:none">Jillian is a <i>USA TODAY</i> bestselling author who writes fun romance novels with characters her readers fall in love with--from the boy next door in the That Boy trilogy, to the daughter of a famous actress in The Keatyn Chronicles®, to a kick-ass young assassin in the Spy Girl® series. Jillian's books have enthralled more than two million readers since she burst onto the indie scene in 2011.<br /><br />She lives in a small Florida beach town, is married to her college sweetheart, has two grown children, and two Labrador Retrievers named Cali and Camber. When she's not working, she likes to travel, paint, shop for shoes, watch football, and go to the beach.<br /><br />Check out Jillian’s website for added content: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jilliandodd.net">www.jilliandodd.net</a><br /><br /></span>
